#+TITLE: nelisp-emacs Doc 33 -- Emacs C-core substrate priority plan for vendor-first replacement
#+AUTHOR: nelisp-emacs
#+DATE: 2026-06-30
#+STATUS: DRAFT
#+DEPENDS_ON: Doc 17 library-first reuse strategy, Doc 22 reader-core gaps, Doc 28 compatibility global API policy, Doc 32 vendored Org bridge policy

* 0. Purpose

This document is a handoff plan for continuing the practical Emacs
replacement track.

The project objective is not to reimplement Dired, Magit, Org, or other
major applications as independent local packages.  The objective is to make
vendored Emacs Lisp and upstream Elisp packages run by implementing the
missing Emacs C-core behavior as reusable =nelisp-emacs= substrate.

Rust dependency reduction is not a project goal for this track.

* 1. Non-negotiable direction

- Vendor and upstream Elisp source is the first implementation target.
- Local code should bridge missing Emacs primitives, runtime behavior, and
  compatibility shims.
- Do not grow independent local Dired, Magit, Org, or transient-like
  implementations when upstream source exists.
- Treat each vendor load failure as evidence of missing substrate until
  proven otherwise.
- Put reusable behavior in the lowest appropriate library owner, not in
  app, GUI, or TUI glue.

* 2. Current progress snapshot

This is an approximate engineering snapshot, not a completion claim.

| Area | Current state |
|------+---------------|
| =text-mode.el= | standalone vendor replay succeeds with =VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=300s= / =VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=260=; representative text-mode surface proof currently takes about 196.77s after real vendor =textmodes/text-mode.el= load. The fix is in the replay substrate: after each replayed file, the harness now extracts provided features from the normalized source and replays explicit =(provide 'feature)= forms so the standalone =require= registry sees features provided during file replay.  Keep this as a resolved provided-feature replay-boundary fix, not a mailto body failure and not local mailto handling |

Approximate overall replacement progress: 35-45%.

Approximate vendor-first milestone progress for core modes plus Magit plus
Org: 20-30%.

* 3. Priority map

** P0. EIEIO and cl-generic

Reason: Magit, transient, and Org-adjacent libraries depend on Emacs object
and generic dispatch behavior.

Core surfaces:

- =defclass=
- =make-instance=
- =eieio-defclass-internal=
- class registry via =cl--find-class=
- =cl-defmethod=
- generic dispatch and method combination
- =cl-typep= over built-in classes, structs, records, and EIEIO classes
- =eieio-object-p=, =object-of-class-p=, =child-of-class-p=

Current blocker shape:

- =transient.el= now reaches the standalone success sentinel through
  =compat.el=, =cond-let.el=, and =llama.el=; the old
  =transient-lisp-variable= stop is no longer current evidence.
- The relevant upstream class shape remains useful as a focused regression:

#+begin_src emacs-lisp
(defclass transient-lisp-variable
  (transient-variable)
  ((reader :initform #'transient-lisp-variable--reader)
   (always-read :initform t)
   (set-value :initarg :set-value :initform #'set)))
#+end_src

- =magit-section.el= now reaches the standalone success sentinel through
  =with-editor.el=.
- =magit-base.el= did not fail at a reported subclass form in the latest
  check; the minimal chain through =magit-section.el= timed out at 600s.
  Continue treating this as an external-vendor replay/performance or deeper
  substrate boundary until a traced run proves a concrete form.
- The replay harness now supports =VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=.
  Use it instead of relying only on GNU =timeout= when reducing long external
  chains, because it reports the last sentinel, keeps diagnostic files on
  internal timeout, and kills the child REPL instead of leaving an orphan.
  A short 10s =magit-base.el= probe currently reports =reader:start=, which
  means the run timed out before the standalone reader reached the first
  vendor load marker.
- A 240s traced probe reaches =with-editor.el= form 66, the
  =cl-defun with-editor-export-editor= form.  A 360s traced probe continues
  past =with-editor.el= and =magit-section.el=, then times out at
  =magit-base.el= form 23.
- A 540s traced probe reaches =magit-base.el= form 25.  A 720s traced probe
  reaches =magit-base.el= form 26.
- In the generated normalized replay, =magit-base.el= forms 21, 23, 24,
  25, and 26 are:

#+begin_src emacs-lisp
(defclass magit-commit-section
  (magit-section)
  ((keymap :initform 'magit-commit-section-map)))

(defclass magit-diff-section
  (magit-section)
  ((keymap :initform 'magit-diff-section-map))
  :abstract t)

(defclass magit-file-section
  (magit-diff-section)
  ((keymap :initform 'magit-file-section-map)
   (source :initform nil :initarg :source)
   (header :initform nil :initarg :header)
   (binary :initform nil :initarg :binary)
   (heading-highlight-face :initform 'magit-diff-file-heading-highlight)
   (heading-selection-face :initform 'magit-diff-file-heading-selection)))

(defclass magit-module-section
  (magit-file-section)
  ((keymap :initform 'magit-module-section-map)
   (range :initform nil :initarg :range)))

(defclass magit-hunk-section
  (magit-diff-section)
  ((keymap :initform 'magit-hunk-section-map)
   (painted :initform nil)
   (fontified :initform nil)
   (refined :initform nil)
   (combined :initform nil :initarg :combined)
   (from-range :initform nil :initarg :from-range)
   (from-ranges :initform nil)
   (to-range :initform nil :initarg :to-range)
   (about :initform nil :initarg :about)
   (heading-highlight-face :initform 'magit-diff-hunk-heading-highlight)
   (heading-selection-face :initform 'magit-diff-hunk-heading-selection)))
#+end_src

- These forms plus the intervening =(setf (alist-get ...))= pass as extracted
  standalone proofs after loading only vendored =eieio.el=, and also after
  the real external-vendor chain through =magit-section.el= has loaded.
  Therefore the next blocker is not these isolated =defclass= shapes; it is
  the cumulative =magit-base.el= replay path after that point, currently
  around form 26 and beyond.
- The normalized forms after form 26 begin with:

#+begin_src emacs-lisp
(defun magit--meta-hunk-p
    (section)
  (not (cdr (oref section value))))

(setf (alist-get 'file magit--section-type-alist)
      'magit-file-section)
(setf (alist-get 'module magit--section-type-alist)
      'magit-module-section)
(setf (alist-get 'hunk magit--section-type-alist)
      'magit-hunk-section)

(defclass magit-log-section
  (magit-section)
  ((keymap :initform 'magit-log-section-map))
  :abstract t)

(defclass magit-unpulled-section (magit-log-section) nil)
(defclass magit-unpushed-section (magit-log-section) nil)
(defclass magit-unmerged-section (magit-log-section) nil)

(setf (alist-get 'unpulled magit--section-type-alist)
      'magit-unpulled-section)
(setf (alist-get 'unmerged magit--section-type-alist)
      'magit-unmerged-section)
#+end_src

  These form 27-39 shapes pass after the real external-vendor chain through
  =magit-section.el= has loaded.  Forms 40-42, the exact normalized bodies of
  =magit-completing-read=, =magit--format-prompt=, and
  =magit--completion-table=, also pass as an extracted proof after the same
  real external-vendor chain.  The proof includes a metadata call through the
  returned =magit--completion-table= lambda.
- Direct checks showed the parent =magit-section= class and its slot vector
  can exist in standalone replay, and the full =magit-section.el= file now
  loads successfully.
- A standalone =eieio.el= proof for a simple parent/child class and a same-slot
  override child passes, so the blocker is not the basic =defclass= macro or
  trivial slot override.  It is likely in deeper vendor EIEIO state:
  parent-chain slot copying, class option propagation, class/default-object
  cache construction, or cl-generic method interaction after Transient/Magit
  class graphs are loaded.
- Continue by isolating the full =defclass= macro expansion path:
  =defalias=, =make-obsolete=, =define-symbol-prop=,
  =eieio-defclass-internal=, constructor =defun=, and any =declare=
  handling.

2026-07-03 resolution: the standalone replay harness now proves the full
=magit-base.el=, =magit-core.el=, and =magit.el= cumulative chains
(283.08s, 520.59s, and 783.77s respectively, each with a
=featurep=/command-surface proof) under the post-perf-fix NeLisp reader
d0321078.  The blocker described above was the NeLisp runtime
allocator/GC scaling boundary, fixed by nelisp commits =0be0e1d6=,
=79550f98=, =a2842b03=, and =5a337c8f= (merged into d0321078), not an
EIEIO substrate defect.  P0's remaining work therefore moves from
cumulative load replay to execution-level proofs: =magit-status= buffer
creation, Git process invocation through the shared process substrate,
and transient menu construction (Doc 33 §4 item 8).

Expected fix location:

- =src/cl-lib.el=
- =src/emacs-cl-macros.el=
- =src/cl-preloaded-shim.el=
- vendor standalone prelude only if the missing behavior is truly reader
  bootstrap-level

Do not patch Magit source to bypass EIEIO.

** P1. Custom, faces, and load-time metadata

Reason: Dired, Magit, transient, Org, and many Emacs libraries load large
amounts of =defcustom=, =defface=, =defgroup=, obsolete metadata, and symbol
properties.

Core surfaces:

- =defgroup=, =defcustom=, =defface=
- =custom-declare-variable=, =custom-declare-face=
- =make-obsolete=, =make-obsolete-variable=
- =define-obsolete-function-alias=, =define-obsolete-variable-alias=
- =put= / =get= symbol metadata consistency
- face inheritance and face spec storage

Acceptance target:

- Vendor packages should be able to load their declarations without
  executing UI customization code or corrupting symbol metadata.

** P2. Keymaps and command loop

Reason: Dired, Magit, transient, and Org are command surfaces.  Loading can
pass while the editor is still unusable if keymaps and command dispatch are
wrong.

Core surfaces:

- sparse keymaps and full keymaps
- =define-key=, =keymap-set=, =keymap-unset=
- parent keymaps and composed maps
- minor-mode maps and local maps
- remapping entries
- =kbd= parsing
- prefix commands
- transient maps and command invocation
- =call-interactively= and command metadata

Acceptance target:

- Vendor Dired keymaps should resolve real commands.
- Transient should be able to construct command menus from upstream source.
- Magit section keymaps should attach without local replacement commands.

** P3. Text properties, overlays, markers, and narrowing

Reason: Magit section UI and Org parsing/editing depend on Emacs buffer
metadata, not just buffer strings.

Core surfaces:

- markers and marker movement on insert/delete
- overlays and overlay properties
- =put-text-property=, =add-text-properties=, =get-text-property=
- =next-single-property-change=, =previous-single-property-change=
- intangible/invisible/display properties where needed by vendor code
- =narrow-to-region=, =widen=, restriction state

Acceptance target:

- Magit sections should be represented using upstream section text
  properties/overlays.
- Org parser and folding should operate on buffer state rather than a
  side-channel local parser.

** P4. Process, files, and Git execution

Reason: Magit and VC are not meaningful without correct process and file
semantics.

Core surfaces:

- =call-process=
- =process-file=
- =start-process=
- process filters and sentinels
- exit status and signal status
- environment variables and =process-environment=
- default-directory handling
- coding systems around process input/output
- =file-attributes=, =directory-files=, symlink and permission behavior

Acceptance target:

- =vc-git.el= should not only load, but execute basic Git queries.
- =magit-status= should be able to run Git commands through upstream Magit
  code paths.

** P5. Window, buffer display, and help surfaces

Reason: Major packages create, select, display, bury, and reuse buffers.

Core surfaces:

- =display-buffer=
- =pop-to-buffer=
- =switch-to-buffer=
- =get-buffer-create=
- selected window / selected buffer interactions
- side-window and reusable-window approximations
- help buffers and quit-window behavior

Acceptance target:

- Dired, Magit status, transient popups, help buffers, and completion buffers
  should use shared display behavior instead of app-local display hacks.

** P6. Minibuffer and completion

Reason: Commands that load but cannot prompt are not usable.

Core surfaces:

- =read-from-minibuffer=
- =completing-read=
- =read-file-name=
- history variables
- default value handling
- completion tables and predicates
- minibuffer maps

Acceptance target:

- Dired file commands, Magit branch/remote/action prompts, and Org capture
  prompts can run through shared minibuffer substrate.

** P7. Syntax, font-lock, search, and regexp match data

Reason: Text modes, Org, Dired, and Magit all depend on accurate search and
highlight behavior.

Core surfaces:

- =re-search-forward=, =looking-at=, =string-match=
- match data, =save-match-data=, =match-string=
- syntax tables and =syntax-propertize=
- font-lock keywords, jit-lock, and face application
- Tree-sitter compatibility stubs where vendor Emacs expects them

Acceptance target:

- Loading Org should not stop on =treesit-font-lock-rules=.
- Font-lock should degrade predictably when the full display engine is not
  present.

** P8. Timers, hooks, advice, and autoloads

Reason: Upstream packages wire themselves together through global Emacs
integration mechanisms.

Core surfaces:

- =add-hook=, =remove-hook=, =run-hooks=
- buffer-local hooks
- =advice-add=, =advice-remove=, =define-advice=
- =autoload=, =autoload-do-load=
- generated autoload forms
- timers and idle timers

Acceptance target:

- Vendor packages should load their integration code without bypassing hook
  or advice behavior.

** P9. Org-specific late prerequisites

Org should remain after core modes and Magit.

Likely prerequisite surfaces:

- narrowing and markers
- text properties and overlays
- regexp/match data fidelity
- font-lock and treesit compatibility
- calendar/time/diary
- tables and alignment
- links and buttons
- agenda file scanning
- capture templates and file writes

Policy:

- Upstream =vendor/emacs-lisp/org/org.el= and =org-element.el= are the
  source of truth.
- Lightweight local Org code may exist only as temporary degraded behavior
  and must not become the main parser.

* 4. Recommended execution order

Magit remains an important proof target, but it is too large to use as the
only day-to-day driver.  Prefer smaller vendor-first substrate gates first,
then return to Magit when the underlying Emacs C-core surfaces have advanced.

1. Finish small P1/P3/P4/P8 substrate pieces exposed by vendored Emacs Lisp:
   obsolete/custom metadata, advertised calling convention metadata, text
   properties, overlays, markers, narrowing, process/file basics, hooks,
   advice, autoloads, and timers.
2. Re-run lightweight vendor replays such as =text-mode.el=, =outline.el=,
   =dired.el=, =dired-x.el=, =vc.el=, =vc-git.el=, =files.el=, and other
   Emacs-distributed libraries before broad external-package checks.
3. The first broad small-gate wave is now documented below and reaches through
   URL/MIME/i18n helpers, facemenu, replace, help/menu/isearch, comint/shell,
   command dispatch, and ibuffer-level surfaces.  Add or reduce more
   Emacs-distributed gates only when they expose an uncovered substrate family
   such as text properties/overlays, file/process behavior, minibuffer
   completion, keymaps/dispatch, package/autoload metadata, or hooks.
   Keep =help.el= as a slower P2/P5 help-surface gate; its representative
   help-map/global-map binding proof currently succeeds in about 148.90s.
   Keep =window.el= as a P5 load gate whose top-level command key wiring is
   intentionally separated from the load proof.
4. Revisit the Magit EIEIO blocker only through focused minimal
   reproductions extracted from the vendor forms.  Do not use full
   =magit.el= as the next routine gate.
5. Prove =magit-base.el= replay.
6. Prove =magit-core.el= replay.
7. Prove =magit.el= load replay without patching Magit source.
8. Move from load proof to minimal command proof:
   - =magit-status= can create/select a status buffer;
   - Git process invocation is routed through shared process substrate;
   - transient command maps can be constructed.
9. Strengthen text property, overlay, marker, and window display behavior
   against the Magit UI path.  DONE 2026-07-04, all slices proven.
   Text-property/section-navigation behavior proved 2026-07-03 against the
   full Magit UI path (§8 item 210).
   Overlay-based highlight behavior, markers, and window display proved
   2026-07-04 through real vendor =magit-section.el=/=magit-base.el= code on
   a self-contained 7-file chain (no full =magit.el= load or git fixture
   needed); see §8 item 216.  The last slice — window scrolling/recentering
   under the full Magit status buffer — proved 2026-07-04 on the full
   85-file =magit.el= chain with the synthetic git fixture (status=done,
   318.79s), after giving =recenter=/=scroll-up=/=scroll-down=/
   =pos-visible-in-window-p= real line-based semantics in
   =src/emacs-window.el= + =src/emacs-window-builtins.el=; see §8 item 218.
10. Re-run Dired, text-mode, outline-mode, VC, and Magit focused replays.
   DONE 2026-07-04: =text-mode.el= (strong proof), =outline.el=,
   =dired.el=, =dired-x.el=, and the =vc.el=/=vc-git.el= chain all
   re-passed under the current multi-chunk-cold-load NeLisp reader with
   the normalized-form cache warm, in 45.59s/42.38s/60.64s/40.19s/54.72s
   respectively; the Magit chains were already re-verified the same day
   at §8 items 216 and 218, so no separate Magit re-run was needed here.
   See §8 item 219.

   2026-07-04 corrections: item 220's honest re-run confirmed the four
   non-Magit legs (outline/dired/dired-x/vc+vc-git) but found the
   =text-mode.el= strong proof genuinely failing.  Item 221 then fixed
   the underlying substrate gaps (=define-derived-mode= backquote bridge,
   =define-minor-mode= fallback gate ordering, =syntax-table-p=,
   =text-mode-hook= pre-binding), after which an equal-free equivalent of
   the strong proof passes (=status=done=, 40.27s).  The ORIGINAL proof
   file's single =(equal ...)= conjunct remains blocked by a reader-side
   stdlib-prelude defect that makes every =equal= call error (minimal
   repro in item 221) -- reader-side fix pending in dev/nelisp.
11. Start upstream Org load only after the above remains stable.  DONE
   2026-07-04: the FULL 60-file upstream Org dependency chain now loads in
   the NeLisp standalone reader (=make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast=,
   status=done, exit=0, elapsed 239.4s, proof
   =(and (featurep 'org) (featurep 'org-element) (fboundp 'org-mode)
   (fboundp 'org-element-parse-buffer) (commandp 'org-mode))=); see §8
   item 215.  Cold-load: see §8 item 217.

   2026-07-04 proof-mechanism correction: the =status=done= above was a
   false positive from a broken proof-scaffold harness bug (§8 item 220).
   Re-run with the fixed harness, the same 5-conjunct proof actually
   FAILS (=featurep org=/=org-element= and =fboundp
   org-element-parse-buffer= hold, but =fboundp=/=commandp org-mode= do
   not), while a reduced 3-conjunct proof (dropping the two =org-mode=
   checks) passes.  So: the Org vendor chain's features/parser genuinely
   load, but installing =org-mode= as a real command is an OPEN gap, not
   DONE.  The normalizer's 3500-char defun truncation/elision lists do
   NOT touch =org-mode= or =define-derived-mode= (checked directly in
   =standalone-source-normalize.el= -- that mechanism only ever matches
   plain =defun= forms); org.el's =(define-derived-mode org-mode
   outline-mode ...)= passes through unmodified as one ~6.2KB single-line
   form.  The likely gap is instead a reader/macro-expansion issue
   specific to =define-derived-mode= calls with a non-nil parent mode
   (also reproduced against =magit-section-mode= and
   =paragraph-indent-text-mode= in §8 items 216/219) -- not attempted
   here.  See §8 item 220 for the full re-run matrix.

   2026-07-04 CLOSED (same day, follow-up pass): §8 item 221 root-caused
   the missing =org-mode= command to the substrate bridge
   =define-derived-mode= macro (=src/emacs-mode.el= /
   =src/emacs-mode-builtins.el=) being written as a backquote template,
   whose invocation the standalone reader silently drops, and rewrote
   both macros backquote-free.  The exact 61-file chain from the honest
   re-run above, with the ORIGINAL 5-conjunct proof, now finishes
   =status=done=, exit=0, elapsed 249.76s.  This item is genuinely DONE.

* 5. Verification gates

Use narrow gates first.

** Host load checks

Host Emacs checks prove source availability and load ordering, not
standalone compatibility.

Example:

#+begin_src sh
emacs -Q --batch \
  -L vendor/compat \
  -L vendor/cond-let \
  -L vendor/llama \
  -L vendor/transient/lisp \
  -L vendor/dash.el \
  -L vendor/with-editor/lisp \
  -L vendor/magit/lisp \
  -L vendor/emacs-lisp \
  -L vendor/emacs-lisp/emacs-lisp \
  -L vendor/emacs-lisp/vc \
  --eval "(progn (require 'magit) (princ (featurep 'magit)))"
#+end_src

** Standalone replay checks

Standalone replay is the real compatibility signal for this track.

Known-good examples should stay green:

#+begin_src sh
make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast \
  VENDOR_FAST_FILES="$(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/textmodes/text-mode.el" \
  VENDOR_FAST_PROOF_FORM_ELISP="(featurep (quote text-mode))"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-text-mode-reduced-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'text-mode)
     (equal text-mode-hook '(text-mode-hook-identify))
     (syntax-table-p text-mode-syntax-table)
     (keymapp text-mode-map)
     (eq text-mode-ispell-word-completion 'completion-at-point)
     (commandp 'text-mode)
     (commandp 'paragraph-indent-text-mode)
     (commandp 'paragraph-indent-minor-mode)
     (fboundp 'toggle-text-mode-auto-fill)
     (fboundp 'center-line))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-radix-tree-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let* ((tree radix-tree-empty)
       (seen nil))
  (setq tree (radix-tree-insert tree "car" 1))
  (setq tree (radix-tree-insert tree "cat" 2))
  (setq tree (radix-tree-insert tree "dog" 3))
  (radix-tree-iter-mappings tree (lambda (key val) (push (cons key val) seen)))
  (and (featurep 'radix-tree)
       (fboundp 'radix-tree-insert)
       (fboundp 'radix-tree-lookup)
       (fboundp 'radix-tree-subtree)
       (fboundp 'radix-tree-prefixes)
       (fboundp 'radix-tree-iter-mappings)
       (fboundp 'radix-tree-count)
       (equal (radix-tree-lookup tree "car") 1)
       (equal (radix-tree-lookup tree "cat") 2)
       (equal (radix-tree-lookup tree "dog") 3)
       (null (radix-tree-lookup tree "cow"))
       (= (radix-tree-count tree) 3)
       (radix-tree-subtree tree "ca")
       (equal (radix-tree-prefixes tree "cartwheel") '(1))
       (equal (sort seen (lambda (a b) (string< (car a) (car b))))
              '(("car" . 1) ("cat" . 2) ("dog" . 3)))))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-text-property-search-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(with-temp-buffer
  (insert "abcdefghi")
  (add-text-properties 2 5 '(face bold marker one))
  (add-text-properties 5 8 '(face italic marker two))
  (goto-char (point-min))
  (let ((first (text-property-search-forward 'face nil nil))
        second back equal-match missing)
    (setq second (text-property-search-forward 'face nil nil))
    (goto-char (point-max))
    (setq back (text-property-search-backward 'face nil nil))
    (goto-char (point-min))
    (setq equal-match (text-property-search-forward 'marker 'two t))
    (setq missing (text-property-search-forward 'marker 'absent t))
    (and (featurep 'text-property-search)
         (fboundp 'text-property-search-forward)
         (fboundp 'text-property-search-backward)
         (fboundp 'prop-match-beginning)
         (fboundp 'prop-match-end)
         (fboundp 'prop-match-value)
         (equal (list (prop-match-beginning first)
                      (prop-match-end first)
                      (prop-match-value first))
                '(2 5 bold))
         (equal (list (prop-match-beginning second)
                      (prop-match-end second)
                      (prop-match-value second))
                '(5 8 italic))
         (equal (list (prop-match-beginning back)
                      (prop-match-end back)
                      (prop-match-value back))
                '(5 8 italic))
         (equal (list (prop-match-beginning equal-match)
                      (prop-match-end equal-match)
                      (prop-match-value equal-match))
                '(5 8 two))
         (null missing))))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-thunk-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'cl-lib)
     (featurep 'thunk)
     (macrop 'thunk-delay)
     (macrop 'thunk-let)
     (macrop 'thunk-let*)
     (fboundp 'thunk-force)
     (fboundp 'thunk-evaluated-p)
     (let* ((count 0)
            (delayed (thunk-delay (setq count (+ count 1)) (* count 10))))
       (and (not (thunk-evaluated-p delayed))
            (= (thunk-force delayed) 10)
            (thunk-evaluated-p delayed)
            (= (thunk-force delayed) 10)
            (= count 1)))
     (let ((count 0))
       (thunk-let ((x (progn (setq count (+ count 1)) 7))
                   (y (progn (setq count (+ count 10)) 3)))
         (and (= x 7)
              (= x 7)
              (= count 1))))
     (let ((count 0))
       (thunk-let* ((x (progn (setq count (+ count 1)) 4))
                    (y (+ x 6)))
         (and (= y 10)
              (= count 1)))))
EOF

  VENDOR_FAST_PROOF_FORM_FILE="$proof"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-rmc-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let* ((choice '(?a "always" "Always continue."))
       (altered (rmc--add-key-description choice))
       (old-completing-read (symbol-function 'completing-read))
       long-wrapper long-helper)
  (unwind-protect
      (progn
        (fset 'completing-read (lambda (&rest _args) "session only"))
        (setq long-wrapper
              (read-multiple-choice "Continue?"
                                    '((?a "always") (?s "session only") (?n "no"))
                                    nil nil t))
        (setq long-helper
              (read-multiple-choice--long-answers
               "Continue?" '((?a "always") (?s "session only") (?n "no"))))
        (and (featurep 'rmc)
             (fboundp 'rmc--add-key-description)
             (fboundp 'rmc--show-help)
             (fboundp 'read-multiple-choice)
             (fboundp 'read-multiple-choice--short-answers)
             (fboundp 'read-multiple-choice--long-answers)
             (equal (car altered) ?a)
             (string-match-p "always" (substring-no-properties (cdr altered)))
             (equal long-wrapper '(?s "session only"))
             (equal long-helper '(?s "session only"))))
    (fset 'completing-read old-completing-read)))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-fileloop-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((old-iterator fileloop--iterator)
      (old-scan fileloop--scan-function)
      (old-operate fileloop--operate-function)
      (old-fresh fileloop--freshly-initialized))
  (unwind-protect
      (progn
        (fileloop-initialize '("one.el" "two.el")
                             (lambda () 'scan-ok)
                             (lambda () 'operate-ok))
        (let ((first (iter-next fileloop--iterator))
              (second (iter-next fileloop--iterator)))
          (and (featurep 'generator)
               (featurep 'fileloop)
               (fboundp 'fileloop-initialize)
               (fboundp 'fileloop-next-file)
               (fboundp 'fileloop-continue)
               (fboundp 'fileloop-initialize-search)
               (fboundp 'fileloop-initialize-replace)
               (fboundp 'fileloop--case-fold)
               (equal first "one.el")
               (equal second "two.el")
               (eq (funcall fileloop--scan-function) 'scan-ok)
               (eq (funcall fileloop--operate-function) 'operate-ok)
               fileloop--freshly-initialized
               (eq (let ((search-upper-case nil)
                         (case-fold-search t))
                     (fileloop--case-fold "abc" 'default))
                   t)
               (null (let ((search-upper-case nil)
                           (case-fold-search t))
                       (fileloop--case-fold "abc" nil)))
               (eq (let ((search-upper-case nil)
                         (case-fold-search nil))
                     (fileloop--case-fold "abc" t))
                   t))))
    (setq fileloop--iterator old-iterator
          fileloop--scan-function old-scan
          fileloop--operate-function old-operate
          fileloop--freshly-initialized old-fresh)))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-help-macro-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((expanded (macroexpand
                 '(make-help-screen nelisp-help-proof-map
                    "a:alpha ?"
                    "Proof %THIS-KEY%"
                    nelisp-help-proof-keymap
                    " *Proof Help*"))))
  (and (featurep 'help-macro)
       (boundp 'three-step-help)
       (boundp 'help-for-help-use-variable-pitch)
       (macrop 'make-help-screen)
       (fboundp 'help--help-screen)
       (eq three-step-help nil)
       (eq help-for-help-use-variable-pitch t)
       (eq (car expanded) 'defun)
       (eq (cadr expanded) 'nelisp-help-proof-map)
       (string= (nth 2 expanded) "Help command.")
       (equal (nth 3 expanded) '(interactive))
       (equal (nth 4 expanded)
              '(help--help-screen "a:alpha ?" "Proof %THIS-KEY%"
                                  nelisp-help-proof-keymap " *Proof Help*"))))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-regi-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(with-temp-buffer
  (insert "alpha\nbeta\nALPHA\n")
  (goto-char (point-min))
  (let ((events nil)
        (frame (list
                '(begin (push 'begin events))
                '("alpha" (push (cons 'alpha curline) events))
                '("beta" (push (cons 'beta curline) events))
                '(every (push 'every events))
                '(end (push 'end events)))))
    (regi-interpret frame (point-min) (point-max))
    (and (featurep 'regi)
         (fboundp 'regi-pos)
         (fboundp 'regi-mapcar)
         (fboundp 'regi-interpret)
         (equal (regi-mapcar '("a" "b") '(push curline events))
                '(("a" (push curline events)) ("b" (push curline events))))
         (member 'begin events)
         (member 'end events)
         (member '(alpha . "alpha") events)
         (member '(beta . "beta") events)
         (>= (length (delq nil (mapcar (lambda (x) (eq x 'every)) events))) 3))))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-generator-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let* ((first (iter-lambda ()
                (iter-yield 1)
                (iter-yield 2)
                'done))
       (second (iter-lambda ()
                 (iter-yield 0)
                 (iter-yield-from (funcall first))
                 (iter-yield 3)
                 'outer-done))
       (it (funcall second))
       values ended)
  (push (iter-next it) values)
  (push (iter-next it) values)
  (push (iter-next it) values)
  (push (iter-next it) values)
  (setq ended (condition-case err
                  (progn (iter-next it) nil)
                (iter-end-of-sequence (cadr err))))
  (and (featurep 'generator)
       (condition-case nil (progn (iter-next iter-empty) nil)
         (iter-end-of-sequence t))
       (macrop 'iter-lambda)
       (macrop 'iter-defun)
       (macrop 'iter-yield-from)
       (fboundp 'iter-yield)
       (fboundp 'iter-next)
       (fboundp 'iter-close)
       (equal (nreverse values) '(0 1 2 3))
       (eq ended 'outer-done)))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-avl-tree-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((tree (avl-tree--create #'<))
      values stack-values)
  (mapc (lambda (x) (avl-tree-enter tree x)) '(5 2 8 1 3 7 9))
  (setq values (avl-tree-flatten tree))
  (avl-tree-delete tree 5)
  (let ((stack (avl-tree-stack tree)))
    (while (not (avl-tree-stack-empty-p stack))
      (push (avl-tree-stack-pop stack) stack-values)))
  (and (featurep 'avl-tree)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree--create)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-p)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-enter)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-delete)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-member)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-member-p)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-mapcar)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-flatten)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-size)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-stack)
       (fboundp 'avl-tree-stack-pop)
       (avl-tree-p tree)
       (equal values '(1 2 3 5 7 8 9))
       (equal (avl-tree-flatten tree) '(1 2 3 7 8 9))
       (= (avl-tree-size tree) 6)
       (eq (avl-tree-member-p tree 7) t)
       (not (avl-tree-member-p tree 5))
       (equal (avl-tree-mapcar (lambda (x) (* x 2)) tree) '(2 4 6 14 16 18))
       (equal (nreverse stack-values) '(1 2 3 7 8 9))))
EOF

(let* ((hex (color-rgb-to-hex 1.0 0.5 0.0 2))
       (hsl (color-rgb-to-hsl 1.0 0.0 0.0))

       (hsv (color-rgb-to-hsv 0.0 1.0 0.0))
       (xyz (color-srgb-to-xyz 1.0 1.0 1.0))
       (lab (color-srgb-to-lab 1.0 1.0 1.0))
       (oklab (color-srgb-to-oklab 1.0 1.0 1.0))
       (clamped (mapcar #'color-clamp '(-0.2 0.4 1.7))))
  (and (featurep 'color)
       (fboundp 'color-rgb-to-hex)
       (fboundp 'color-rgb-to-hsl)
       (fboundp 'color-hsl-to-rgb)

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-composite-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let* ((rule '(br tc 10 -20))
       (code (encode-composition-rule rule))
       (decoded (decode-composition-rule code))
       (components (vector ?A '(br . tc) ?B '(tc . bl) ?C))
       (encoded-components (encode-composition-components components))
       (decoded-components (decode-composition-components encoded-components))
       (glyph (vector 1 2 ?A 65 7 -1 2 9 3 nil))
       (glyph-copy nil)
       (gstring (vector (vector 'font ?A ?B) nil glyph)))
  (lglyph-set-adjustment glyph 1 2 3)
  (setq glyph-copy (lglyph-copy glyph))
  (and (featurep 'composite)
       (boundp 'reference-point-alist)
       (fboundp 'encode-composition-rule)
       (fboundp 'decode-composition-rule)
       (fboundp 'encode-composition-components)
       (fboundp 'decode-composition-components)
       (fboundp 'lgstring-header)
       (fboundp 'lgstring-char-len)
       (fboundp 'lgstring-glyph-len)
       (fboundp 'lglyph-char)
       (fboundp 'lglyph-set-adjustment)
       (integerp code)
       (equal decoded '(br 10 -20 tc))
       (integerp (aref encoded-components 1))
       (integerp (aref encoded-components 3))
       (equal decoded-components components)
       (eq (lgstring-font gstring) 'font)
       (= (lgstring-char-len gstring) 2)
       (= (lgstring-glyph-len gstring) 1)
       (= (lglyph-from glyph) 1)
       (= (lglyph-to glyph) 2)
       (eq (lglyph-char glyph) ?A)
       (= (lglyph-code glyph) 65)
       (= (lglyph-width glyph) 7)
       (equal (lglyph-adjustment glyph) [1 2 3])
       (equal glyph-copy glyph)))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-battery-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(defun nelisp-battery-proof-status ()
  '((?L . "AC") (?B . "ok") (?b . "+") (?p . "88") (?t . "1:23")))
(let ((battery-status-function #'nelisp-battery-proof-status)
      (battery-mode-line-format "[%b%p%% %t]")
      (battery-echo-area-format "Power %L %p%%")
      (battery-update-functions nil)
      (battery-update-interval 999)
      (battery-mode-line-limit 100)
      (battery-update-timer nil)
      (global-mode-string nil)
      formatted ok)
  (unwind-protect
      (progn
        (setq formatted (battery-format battery-echo-area-format
                                        (nelisp-battery-proof-status)))
        (setq ok
              (and (featurep 'battery)
                   (commandp 'battery)
                   (commandp 'display-battery-mode)
                   (fboundp 'battery-format)
                   (fboundp 'battery-update)
                   (fboundp 'battery-update-handler)
                   (fboundp 'battery--files)
                   (fboundp 'battery--find-linux-sysfs-batteries)
                   (string= formatted "Power AC 88%")))
        (battery-update)
        (setq ok (and ok (string= battery-mode-line-string "[+88% 1:23]")))
        ok)
    (when battery-update-timer
      (ignore-errors (cancel-timer battery-update-timer)))))
EOF

     (fboundp 'tty-color-clear)
     (fboundp 'tty-color-translate)
     (fboundp 'tty-color-values)
     (fboundp 'tty-color-desc)
     (fboundp 'tty-color-by-index)
     (fboundp 'tty-color-standard-values)
     (fboundp 'tty-color-approximate)
     (fboundp 'tty-color-gray-shades)
     (let ((tty-defined-color-alist nil))
       (tty-color-define "proof-red" 1 '(65535 0 0))
       (and (equal (tty-color-standard-values "red") '(65535 0 0))
            (equal (tty-color-translate "proof-red") 1)
            (equal (tty-color-values "proof-red") '(65535 0 0))
            (equal (tty-color-by-index 1) "proof-red")
            (consp (tty-color-desc "red"))
            (integerp (tty-color-approximate '(65000 0 0)))
            (integerp (tty-color-gray-shades))))))

       (member "black" x-colors)
       (member "white" x-colors)

       (equal (cdr (assq 'border-width default-frame-alist)) 9)

       (equal (cdr (assq 'charset khmer)) '(unicode))
       (equal (cdr (assq 'coding-system khmer)) '(utf-8))

       (vectorp (car khmer-composition))
       (string-match-p "1780" (aref (car khmer-composition) 0))

       extended-composition
       (equal main-composition extended-composition)
       (vectorp (car main-composition))
       (vectorp (cadr main-composition))
       (equal (aref (car main-composition) 0) burmese-composable-pattern)
       (equal (aref (cadr main-composition) 0) ".")

       lao-info
       (coding-system-p 'lao)
       (eq (cdr (assq 'charset lao-info)) 'lao)
       (equal (cdr (assq 'coding-system lao-info)) '(lao))
       (equal (cdr (assq 'coding-priority lao-info)) '(lao))
       (equal (cdr (assq 'input-method lao-info)) "lao")
       (eq (cdr (assq 'unibyte-display lao-info)) 'lao)
       (equal (cdr (assq 'features lao-info)) '(lao-util))
       upper
       tone
       lower
       (vectorp (car upper))
       (vectorp (car tone))
       (vectorp (car lower))
       (eq (aref (car upper) 2) 'lao-composition-function)
       (eq (aref (car tone) 2) 'lao-composition-function)
       (eq (aref (car lower) 2) 'lao-composition-function)))
EOF
VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=180s \
VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=150 \

     (assoc "zhong" pinyin-character-map)
     (assoc "ri" pinyin-character-map)
     (assoc "nv" pinyin-character-map)
     (string-match-p "中" (cdr (assoc "zhong" pinyin-character-map)))
     (string-match-p "日" (cdr (assoc "ri" pinyin-character-map)))
     (string-match-p "女" (cdr (assoc "nv" pinyin-character-map))))
EOF

  VENDOR_FAST_PROOF_FORM_ELISP="(and (featurep (quote mail-prsvr)) (featurep (quote mm-util)) (featurep (quote utf7)) (fboundp (quote utf7-encode)) (fboundp (quote utf7-decode)) (fboundp (quote utf7-get-u16char-converter)) (fboundp (quote mm-coding-system-p)) (macrop (quote mm-with-multibyte-buffer)) (macrop (quote mm-with-unibyte-buffer)))"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-robin-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((pkg "nelisp-robin")
      (input (apply 'string '(97 98 32 97 99 100 32 120)))
      (expected (apply 'string '(913 32 916 32 120))))
  (and (featurep 'robin)
       (macrop 'robin-define-package)
       (fboundp 'robin-convert-region)
       (fboundp 'robin-convert-buffer)
       (fboundp 'robin-invert-region)
       (fboundp 'robin-modify-package)
       (fboundp 'robin-use-package)
       (progn
         (robin-define-package "nelisp-robin" "NeLisp Robin proof"
           ("ab" ?Α)
           ("acd" ?Δ)
           ("x" "x"))
         t)
       (assoc pkg robin-package-alist)
       (equal (get-char-code-property ?Α 'nelisp-robin) "ab")
       (with-temp-buffer
         (insert input)
         (robin-convert-region (point-min) (point-max) pkg)
         (and (equal (buffer-string) expected)
              (robin-invert-region (point-min) (point-max) pkg)
              (equal (buffer-string) input)))))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-time-stamp-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((sample (time-stamp-string "%Y-%02m-%02d"))
      (time-stamp-format "%Y-%02m-%02d")
      (time-stamp-pattern nil)
      (time-stamp-line-limit 8)
      (time-stamp-count 1)
      (time-stamp-active t)
      (time-stamp-warn-inactive nil))
  (and (featurep 'time-stamp)
       (commandp 'time-stamp)
       (commandp 'time-stamp-toggle-active)
       (fboundp 'time-stamp-string)
       (fboundp 'time-stamp-string-preprocess)
       (fboundp 'time-stamp-once)
       (fboundp 'time-stamp-zone-type-p)
       (fboundp 'time-stamp--format)
       (boundp 'time-stamp-format)
       (boundp 'time-stamp-start)
       (boundp 'time-stamp-end)
       (boundp 'time-stamp-line-limit)
       (stringp sample)
       (string-match-p "^[0-9][0-9][0-9][0-9]-[0-9][0-9]-[0-9][0-9]$" sample)
       (with-temp-buffer
         (insert "Time-stamp: <>\nbody\n")
         (goto-char (point-min))
         (time-stamp)
         (goto-char (point-min))
         (re-search-forward "Time-stamp: <[0-9][0-9][0-9][0-9]-[0-9][0-9]-[0-9][0-9]>" nil t))
       (let ((time-stamp-active t))
         (time-stamp-toggle-active -1)
         (not time-stamp-active))
       (let ((time-stamp-active nil))
         (time-stamp-toggle-active 1)
         time-stamp-active)))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-autoinsert-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((auto-insert-alist nil)
      (find-file-hook nil))
  (and (featurep 'seq)
       (featurep 'autoinsert)
       (commandp 'auto-insert)
       (commandp 'auto-insert-mode)
       (fboundp 'define-auto-insert)
       (boundp 'auto-insert)
       (boundp 'auto-insert-query)
       (boundp 'auto-insert-prompt)
       (boundp 'auto-insert-alist)
       (boundp 'auto-insert-directory)
       (progn
         (define-auto-insert "\\.foo\\'" "foo-template")
         (equal (cdr (assoc "\\.foo\\'" auto-insert-alist)) "foo-template"))
       (progn
         (define-auto-insert "\\.foo\\'" "bar-template" t)
         (let ((entry (cdr (assoc "\\.foo\\'" auto-insert-alist))))
           (and (vectorp entry)
                (= (length entry) 2)
                (equal (aref entry 0) "foo-template")
                (equal (aref entry 1) "bar-template"))))
       (progn
         (auto-insert-mode 1)
         (memq 'auto-insert find-file-hook))
       (progn
         (auto-insert-mode -1)
         (not (memq 'auto-insert find-file-hook)))))
EOF

              (progn
                (word-wrap-whitespace-mode -1)
                (and (not word-wrap-whitespace-mode)
                     (eq (category-table) initial-table)))))))
EOF

  VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=220s \
  VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=190 \
  VENDOR_FAST_FILES="$(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/textmodes/word-wrap-mode.el" \
  VENDOR_FAST_PROOF_FORM_FILE="$proof"
rm -f "$proof"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-page-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'page)
     (commandp 'forward-page)
     (commandp 'backward-page)
     (commandp 'mark-page)
     (commandp 'narrow-to-page)
     (commandp 'count-lines-page)
     (commandp 'what-page)
     (fboundp 'page--count-lines-page)
     (fboundp 'page--what-page)
     (eq (get 'narrow-to-page 'disabled) t)
     (with-temp-buffer
       (let ((page-delimiter "^\f"))
         (insert "one\ntwo\n\f\nthree\nfour\n\f\nfive\n")
         (goto-char (point-min))
         (forward-page 1)
         (let ((p1 (point))
               (w1 (page--what-page)))
           (forward-page 1)
           (let ((p2 (point)))
             (backward-page 1)
             (and (> p1 (point-min))
                  (> p2 p1)
                  (= (point) p1)
                  (equal w1 '(1 0))
                  (progn
                    (goto-char (point-min))
                    (forward-line 1)
                    (equal (page--count-lines-page) '(2 1 1)))))))))
EOF

             (c (repos-count-screen-lines-signed (point-max) (point-min))))
         (and (integerp a)
              (integerp b)
              (integerp c)

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-mailheader-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let* ((headers '((from . "alice@example.test")
                  (subject . "Hello")
                  (x-extra . "One")))
       (parsed (mail-header-parse '((subject . (lambda (s) (list (upcase s) (length s)))))
                                  (copy-tree headers)))
       (merged (mail-header-merge '((subject . (concat (mail-header 'subject) " world"))
                                     (x-new . "created"))
                                  headers)))
  (and (featurep 'mailheader)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-extract)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-extract-no-properties)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-parse)
       (fboundp 'mail-header)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-set)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-merge)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-format)
       (functionp mail-header-format-function)
       (equal (mail-header 'subject headers) "Hello")
       (equal (progn (mail-header-set 'subject "Changed" headers)
                     (mail-header 'subject headers))
              "Changed")
       (equal (cdr (assq 'subject parsed)) '("Hello" "HELLO" 5))
       (equal merged '((subject . "Changed world") (x-new . "created")))
       (with-temp-buffer
         (insert "From: Alice <alice@example.test>\nSubject: Hello\n folded\n\nBody")
         (goto-char (point-min))
         (equal (mail-header-extract)
                '((from . "Alice <alice@example.test>") (subject . "Hello folded"))))
       (with-temp-buffer
         (mail-header-format '((subject) (from) (t)) headers)
         (equal (buffer-string)
                "Subject: Changed\nFrom: alice@example.test\nX-extra: One\n\n"))))
EOF

cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((ob (make-vector 7 0))
      (seen nil))
  (and (featurep 'obarray)
       (boundp 'obarray-default-size)
       (= obarray-default-size 4)
       (fboundp 'obarray-size)
       (fboundp 'obarray-get)
       (fboundp 'obarray-put)
       (fboundp 'obarray-remove)
       (fboundp 'obarray-map)
       (= (obarray-size ob) 4)
       (null (obarray-get ob "alpha"))
       (let ((sym (obarray-put ob "alpha")))
         (and (symbolp sym)
              (eq sym (obarray-get ob "alpha"))
              (eq sym (intern-soft "alpha" ob))))
       (let ((sym (obarray-put ob "beta")))
         (and (symbolp sym)
              (obarray-map (lambda (s) (setq seen (cons (symbol-name s) seen))) ob)
              (member "alpha" seen)
              (member "beta" seen)))
       (obarray-remove ob "alpha")
       (null (obarray-get ob "alpha"))
       (obarray-get ob "beta")))
EOF

  (let ((intangible-at-2 (cursor-sensor--intangible-p 2))
        (intangible-at-1 (cursor-sensor--intangible-p 1))
        intangible-hook-on intangible-hook-off
        sensor-post-on sensor-pre-on sensor-post-off sensor-pre-off)
    (cursor-intangible-mode 1)
    (setq intangible-hook-on (memq 'cursor-sensor--move-to-tangible
                                   pre-redisplay-functions))

                                         pre-redisplay-functions)))

    (setq sensor-post-on (memq 'cursor-sensor--detect post-command-hook)
          sensor-pre-on (memq 'cursor-sensor--detect pre-redisplay-functions))
    (cursor-sensor-mode 0)
    (setq sensor-post-off (not (memq 'cursor-sensor--detect post-command-hook))
          sensor-pre-off (not (memq 'cursor-sensor--detect pre-redisplay-functions)))
    (and (featurep 'easy-mmode)
         (featurep 'cursor-sensor)
         (boundp 'cursor-sensor-inhibit)
         (fboundp 'cursor-sensor--intangible-p)
         (fboundp 'cursor-sensor-tangible-pos)
         (fboundp 'cursor-sensor-move-to-tangible)
         (fboundp 'cursor-sensor--move-to-tangible)
         (fboundp 'cursor-sensor--detect)
         (fboundp 'cursor-intangible-mode)
         (fboundp 'cursor-sensor-mode)
         (commandp 'cursor-intangible-mode)
         (commandp 'cursor-sensor-mode)
         intangible-at-2
         (null intangible-at-1)
         intangible-hook-on
         intangible-hook-off
         sensor-post-on
         sensor-pre-on
         sensor-post-off
         sensor-pre-off)))
EOF

  VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=260s \
  VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=230 \
  VENDOR_FAST_FILES="$(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/calendar/time-date.el $(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/calendar/iso8601.el"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-iso8601-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'time-date)
     (featurep 'iso8601)
     (fboundp 'iso8601-parse)
     (fboundp 'iso8601-parse-date)
     (fboundp 'iso8601-parse-time)
     (fboundp 'iso8601-parse-zone)
     (fboundp 'iso8601-valid-p)
     (fboundp 'iso8601-parse-duration)
     (fboundp 'iso8601-parse-interval)
     (iso8601-valid-p "2020-01-15T16:12:21Z")
     (not (iso8601-valid-p "not-a-date"))
     (let ((dt (iso8601-parse "2020-01-15T16:12:21-08:00")))
       (and (= (decoded-time-second dt) 21)
            (= (decoded-time-minute dt) 12)
            (= (decoded-time-hour dt) 16)
            (= (decoded-time-day dt) 15)
            (= (decoded-time-month dt) 1)
            (= (decoded-time-year dt) 2020)
            (= (decoded-time-zone dt) -28800)))
     (let ((date (iso8601-parse-date "2020-123")))
       (and (= (decoded-time-year date) 2020)
            (= (decoded-time-month date) 5)
            (= (decoded-time-day date) 2)))
     (let ((time (iso8601-parse-time "16:12:21Z")))
       (and (= (decoded-time-hour time) 16)
            (= (decoded-time-minute time) 12)
            (= (decoded-time-second time) 21)
            (= (decoded-time-zone time) 0)))
     (= (iso8601-parse-zone "-08:30") -510)
     (let ((dur (iso8601-parse-duration "P1Y2M3DT4H5M6S")))
       (and (= (decoded-time-year dur) 1)
            (= (decoded-time-month dur) 2)
            (= (decoded-time-day dur) 3)
            (= (decoded-time-hour dur) 4)
            (= (decoded-time-minute dur) 5)
            (= (decoded-time-second dur) 6)))
     (let ((interval (iso8601-parse-interval "2020-01-01/2020-01-02")))
       (and (consp interval)
            (= (decoded-time-day (car interval)) 1)
            (= (decoded-time-day (cdr interval)) 2))))
EOF
make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast \
  VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=260s \
  VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=230 \

  VENDOR_FAST_PROOF_FORM_FILE="$proof"
rm -f "$proof"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-parse-time-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'time-date)
     (featurep 'iso8601)
     (featurep 'parse-time)
     (fboundp 'parse-time-tokenize)
     (fboundp 'parse-time-string)
     (fboundp 'parse-iso8601-time-string)
     (fboundp 'iso8601-parse)
     (equal (parse-time-tokenize "Wed, 15 Jan 2020 16:12:21 -0800")
            '("wed" 15 "jan" 2020 16 12 21 "-0800"))
     (let ((iso (parse-time-string "2020-01-15T16:12:21-08:00")))
       (and (= (nth 0 iso) 21)
            (= (nth 1 iso) 12)
            (= (nth 2 iso) 16)
            (= (nth 3 iso) 15)
            (= (nth 4 iso) 1)
            (= (nth 5 iso) 2020)
            (= (nth 8 iso) -28800)))
     (let ((rfc (parse-time-string "Wed, 15 Jan 2020 16:12:21 -0800")))
       (and (= (nth 0 rfc) 21)
            (= (nth 1 rfc) 12)
            (= (nth 2 rfc) 16)
            (= (nth 3 rfc) 15)
            (= (nth 4 rfc) 1)
            (= (nth 5 rfc) 2020)
            (= (nth 6 rfc) 3)
            (= (nth 8 rfc) -28800)))
     (let ((encoded (parse-iso8601-time-string "2020-01-15T16:12:21Z")))
       (and encoded
            (equal (format-time-string "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S%z" encoded t)
                   "2020-01-15T16:12:21+0000"))))
EOF
make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast \

  VENDOR_FAST_PROOF_FORM_FILE="$proof"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-password-cache-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((password-cache t)
      (password-cache-expiry nil)
      (password-data (make-hash-table :test #'equal)))
  (and (featurep 'password-cache)
       (boundp 'password-cache)
       (boundp 'password-cache-expiry)
       (hash-table-p password-data)
       (fboundp 'password-read-from-cache)
       (fboundp 'password-in-cache-p)
       (fboundp 'password-read)
       (fboundp 'password-cache-add)
       (fboundp 'password-cache-remove)
       (fboundp 'password-reset)
       (null (password-read-from-cache "key"))
       (not (password-in-cache-p "key"))
       (null (password-cache-add "key" "secret"))
       (password-in-cache-p "key")
       (equal (password-read-from-cache "key") "secret")
       (progn (password-cache-remove "key")
              (not (password-in-cache-p "key")))
       (progn (password-cache-add "a" "one")
              (password-cache-add "b" "two")
              (password-reset)
              (and (not (password-in-cache-p "a"))
                   (not (password-in-cache-p "b"))))))
EOF

            (numberp (nth 0 result))

     (let ((result (benchmark-run 1 (+ 1 2))))
       (and (listp result)
            (= (length result) 3)
            (numberp (nth 0 result))
            (integerp (nth 1 result))
            (numberp (nth 2 result))))
     (= (benchmark-progn (+ 1 2)) 3))

cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'ring)
     (fboundp 'make-ring)
     (fboundp 'ring-p)
     (fboundp 'ring-insert)
     (fboundp 'ring-ref)
     (fboundp 'ring-remove)
     (fboundp 'ring-elements)
     (fboundp 'ring-resize)
     (fboundp 'ring-convert-sequence-to-ring)
     (let ((ring (make-ring 3)))
       (and (ring-p ring)
            (= (ring-size ring) 3)
            (ring-empty-p ring)
            (progn
              (ring-insert ring 'a)
              (ring-insert ring 'b)
              (ring-insert ring 'c)
              (and (= (ring-length ring) 3)
                   (eq (ring-ref ring 0) 'c)
                   (eq (ring-ref ring 1) 'b)
                   (equal (ring-elements ring) '(c b a))
                   (= (ring-member ring 'b) 1)
                   (eq (ring-next ring 'c) 'b)
                   (eq (ring-previous ring 'b) 'c)
                   (eq (ring-remove ring 1) 'b)
                   (equal (ring-elements ring) '(c a))
                   (progn
                     (ring-insert+extend ring 'd t)
                     (ring-insert+extend ring 'e t)
                     (and (= (ring-size ring) 4)
                          (equal (ring-elements ring) '(e d c a)))))))))
     (let ((ring (ring-convert-sequence-to-ring [x y z])))
       (and (ring-p ring)
            (= (ring-length ring) 3)
            (equal (ring-elements ring) '(x y z)))))
EOF

     (fboundp 'ntlm-ascii2unicode)
     (fboundp 'ntlm-unicode2ascii)
     (fboundp 'ntlm-md4hash)
     (fboundp 'ntlm-smb-passwd-hash)
     (equal (ntlm-ascii2unicode "User" 4)
            (string ?U 0 ?s 0 ?e 0 ?r 0))
     (equal (encode-hex-string (ntlm-md4hash "password"))
            "8846f7eaee8fb117ad06bdd830b7586c")
     (let ((req (ntlm-build-auth-request "User" "DOMAIN")))
       (and (stringp req)
            (> (length req) 32)
            (equal (substring req 0 8) (concat "NTLMSSP" (string 0))))))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-sasl-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'sasl)
     (featurep 'sasl-plain)
     (featurep 'sasl-login)
     (featurep 'sasl-anonymous)
     (fboundp 'sasl-make-client)
     (fboundp 'sasl-make-mechanism)
     (fboundp 'sasl-next-step)
     (fboundp 'sasl-client-set-property)
     (fboundp 'sasl-client-property)
     (fboundp 'sasl-plain-response)
     (fboundp 'sasl-anonymous-response)
     (let ((plain (get 'sasl-plain 'sasl-mechanism))
           (anonymous (get 'sasl-anonymous 'sasl-mechanism))
           (sasl-read-passphrase (lambda (_prompt) (copy-sequence "secret"))))
       (and (vectorp plain)
            (vectorp anonymous)
            (equal (sasl-mechanism-name plain) "PLAIN")
            (equal (sasl-mechanism-name anonymous) "ANONYMOUS")
            (= (length (sasl-mechanism-steps plain)) 1)
            (= (length (sasl-mechanism-steps anonymous)) 2)
            (let* ((client (sasl-make-client plain "user" "imap" "example.test"))
                   (_ (sasl-client-set-property client 'authenticator-name "authz"))
                   (plain-step (sasl-next-step client nil))
                   (plain-data (sasl-step-data plain-step))
                   (anon-client (sasl-make-client anonymous "anonymous" "imap" "example.test"))
                   (_ (sasl-client-set-property anon-client 'trace "trace-token"))
                   (anon-step1 (sasl-next-step anon-client nil))
                   (anon-step2 (sasl-next-step anon-client anon-step1)))
              (and (equal (sasl-client-name client) "user")
                   (equal (sasl-client-service client) "imap")
                   (equal (sasl-client-server client) "example.test")
                   (equal (sasl-client-property client 'authenticator-name) "authz")
                   (equal plain-data (concat "authz" (string 0) "user" (string 0) "secret"))
                   (vectorp anon-step1)
                   (vectorp anon-step2)
                   (equal (sasl-step-data anon-step2) "trace-token"))))))
EOF
make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast \

     (let ((mechanism (get 'sasl-ntlm 'sasl-mechanism)))
       (and (vectorp mechanism)
            (equal (sasl-mechanism-name mechanism) "NTLM")
            (= (length (sasl-mechanism-steps mechanism)) 3)
            (let* ((client (sasl-make-client mechanism "User" "imap" "example.test"))
                   (step1 (sasl-next-step client nil))
                   (step2 (sasl-next-step client step1))
                   (request (sasl-step-data step2)))
              (and (vectorp step1)
                   (vectorp step2)
                   (stringp request)
                   (> (length request) 32)
                   (equal (substring request 0 8) (concat "NTLMSSP" (string 0))))))))

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-sasl-cram-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'sasl)
     (featurep 'hmac-def)
     (featurep 'hex-util)
     (featurep 'hmac-md5)
     (featurep 'sasl-cram)
     (boundp 'sasl-cram-md5-steps)
     (fboundp 'sasl-cram-md5-response)
     (let ((mechanism (get 'sasl-cram 'sasl-mechanism))
           (sasl-read-passphrase (lambda (_prompt) (copy-sequence "tanstaaft"))))
       (and (vectorp mechanism)
            (equal (sasl-mechanism-name mechanism) "CRAM-MD5")
            (= (length (sasl-mechanism-steps mechanism)) 2)
            (let* ((client (sasl-make-client mechanism "tim" "imap" "example.test"))
                   (step1 (sasl-next-step client nil))
                   (challenge "<1896.697170952@postoffice.reston.mci.net>")
                   (step2 (sasl-next-step client (vector (aref step1 0) challenge)))
                   (response (sasl-step-data step2)))
              (and (vectorp step1)
                   (vectorp step2)
                   (equal response "tim b913a602c7eda7a495b4e6e7334d3890"))))))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-sasl-digest-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'sasl)
     (featurep 'hmac-def)
     (featurep 'hex-util)
     (featurep 'hmac-md5)
     (featurep 'sasl-digest)
     (boundp 'sasl-digest-md5-steps)
     (fboundp 'sasl-digest-md5-parse-string)
     (fboundp 'sasl-digest-md5-digest-uri)
     (fboundp 'sasl-digest-md5-response-value)
     (fboundp 'sasl-digest-md5-response)
     (equal (sasl-digest-md5-digest-uri "imap" "example.test") "imap/example.test")
     (let ((parsed (sasl-digest-md5-parse-string "realm=example.test,nonce=abc,qop=auth")))
       (and (equal (plist-get parsed 'realm) 'example.test)
            (equal (plist-get parsed 'nonce) 'abc)
            (equal (plist-get parsed 'qop) 'auth)))
     (let ((mechanism (get 'sasl-digest 'sasl-mechanism))
           (sasl-read-passphrase (lambda (_prompt) (copy-sequence "secret"))))
       (and (vectorp mechanism)
            (equal (sasl-mechanism-name mechanism) "DIGEST-MD5")
            (= (length (sasl-mechanism-steps mechanism)) 3)
            (let* ((client (sasl-make-client mechanism "user" "imap" "example.test"))
                   (_ (sasl-client-set-property client 'realm "example.test"))
                   (_ (sasl-client-set-property client 'cnonce "fixed-cnonce"))
                   (_ (sasl-client-set-property client 'nonce-count 1))
                   (step1 (sasl-next-step client nil))
                   (challenge "realm=example.test,nonce=abc,qop=auth")
                   (step2 (sasl-next-step client (vector (aref step1 0) challenge)))
                   (response (sasl-step-data step2)))
              (and (vectorp step1)
                   (vectorp step2)
                   (stringp response)
                   (string-match "username=\"user\"" response)
                   (string-match "realm=\"example.test\"" response)
                   (string-match "nonce=\"abc\"" response)
                   (string-match "cnonce=\"fixed-cnonce\"" response)
                   (string-match "nc=00000001" response)
                   (string-match "digest-uri=\"imap/example.test\"" response)
                   (string-match "qop=auth" response)
                   (string-match "response=[0-9a-f]+" response))))))
EOF
make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast \
  VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=220s \
  VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=190 \
  VENDOR_FAST_FILES="$(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/net/sasl.el $(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/net/hmac-def.el $(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/hex-util.el $(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/net/hmac-md5.el $(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/net/sasl-digest.el" \
  VENDOR_FAST_PROOF_FORM_FILE="$proof"

make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast \
  VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=220s \
  VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=190 \
  VENDOR_FAST_FILES="$(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/net/sasl.el $(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/hex-util.el $(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/net/rfc2104.el $(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/net/sasl-scram-rfc.el $(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/net/sasl-scram-sha256.el"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-sasl-scram-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(and (featurep 'sasl)
     (featurep 'hex-util)
     (featurep 'rfc2104)
     (featurep 'sasl-scram-sha-1)
     (featurep 'sasl-scram-rfc)
     (featurep 'sasl-scram-sha256)
     (fboundp 'sasl-scram-client-first-message)
     (fboundp 'sasl-scram-sha-1-client-final-message)
     (fboundp 'sasl-scram-sha-256-client-final-message)
     (fboundp 'sasl-scram-sha256)
     (boundp 'sasl-scram-sha-1-steps)
     (boundp 'sasl-scram-sha-256-steps)
     (let ((sha1-mech (get 'sasl-scram-sha-1 'sasl-mechanism))
           (sha256-mech (get 'sasl-scram-sha256 'sasl-mechanism))
           (sasl-unique-id-function (lambda () "clientnonce"))
           (sasl-read-passphrase (lambda (_prompt) (copy-sequence "pencil"))))
       (and (vectorp sha1-mech)
            (vectorp sha256-mech)
            (equal (sasl-mechanism-name sha1-mech) "SCRAM-SHA-1")
            (equal (sasl-mechanism-name sha256-mech) "SCRAM-SHA-256")
            (= (length (sasl-mechanism-steps sha1-mech)) 3)
            (= (length (sasl-mechanism-steps sha256-mech)) 3)
            (let* ((client1 (sasl-make-client sha1-mech "user" "imap" "example.test"))
                   (first1 (sasl-next-step client1 nil))
                   (server-first "r=clientnonceSERVER,s=c2FsdA==,i=1")
                   (final1 (sasl-next-step client1 (vector (aref first1 0) server-first)))
                   (final1-data (sasl-step-data final1))
                   (client2 (sasl-make-client sha256-mech "user" "imap" "example.test"))
                   (first2 (sasl-next-step client2 nil))
                   (final2 (sasl-next-step client2 (vector (aref first2 0) server-first)))
                   (final2-data (sasl-step-data final2)))
              (and (equal (sasl-step-data first1) "n,,n=user,r=clientnonce")
                   (equal (sasl-step-data first2) "n,,n=user,r=clientnonce")
                   (string-prefix-p "c=biws,r=clientnonceSERVER,p=" final1-data)
                   (string-prefix-p "c=biws,r=clientnonceSERVER,p=" final2-data)
                   (sasl-client-property client1 'auth-message)
                   (sasl-client-property client1 'salted-password)
                   (sasl-client-property client2 'auth-message)
                   (sasl-client-property client2 'salted-password))))))
EOF

(and (featurep 'ietf-drums)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-token-to-list)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-remove-comments)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-remove-whitespace)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-get-comment)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-strip)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-strip-cte)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-parse-address)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-parse-addresses)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-quote-string)
     (fboundp 'ietf-drums-make-address)
     (boundp 'ietf-drums-text-token)
     (boundp 'ietf-drums-tspecials)
     (boundp 'ietf-drums-no-ws-ctl-token)
     (equal (ietf-drums-token-to-list "A-C") '(?A ?B ?C))
     (equal (ietf-drums-remove-comments "alpha (comment) beta") "alpha  beta")
     (equal (ietf-drums-remove-whitespace "a \t\r\n b") "ab")
     (equal (ietf-drums-get-comment "alpha (one) beta (two)") "two")
     (equal (ietf-drums-strip "  hello (ignored) \t") "hello")
     (equal (ietf-drums-strip-cte " quoted-printable (comment) ") "quoted-printable")
     (equal (ietf-drums-quote-string "simple") "simple")
     (equal (ietf-drums-quote-string "two words") "\"two words\"")
     (equal (ietf-drums-make-address "User Name" "user@example.test")
            "\"User Name\" <user@example.test>")
     (equal (ietf-drums-parse-address "User Name <user@example.test>")
            '("user@example.test" . "User Name"))
     (equal (ietf-drums-parse-addresses "One <one@example.test>, Two <two@example.test>")
            '(("one@example.test" . "One") ("two@example.test" . "Two"))))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-mail-parse-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((parsed (mail-header-parse-content-type "text/plain; charset=utf-8; filename*=us-ascii''hello%20world.txt")))
  (and (featurep 'mail-prsvr)
       (featurep 'ietf-drums)
       (featurep 'rfc2045)
       (featurep 'rfc2047)
       (featurep 'rfc2231)
       (featurep 'mail-parse)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-parse-content-type)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-parse-content-disposition)
       (fboundp 'mail-content-type-get)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-encode-parameter)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-remove-comments)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-strip)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-strip-cte)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-parse-address)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-parse-addresses)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-parse-address-lax)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-parse-addresses-lax)
       (fboundp 'mail-header-make-address)
       (equal (mail-content-type-get parsed 'type) "text/plain")
       (equal (mail-content-type-get parsed 'charset) "utf-8")
       (equal (mail-content-type-get parsed 'filename) "hello world.txt")
       (equal (mail-header-remove-comments "alpha (comment) beta") "alpha  beta")
       (equal (mail-header-strip "  hello (ignored) \t") "hello")
       (equal (mail-header-strip-cte " quoted-printable (comment) ") "quoted-printable")
       (equal (mail-header-make-address "User Name" "user@example.test")
              "\"User Name\" <user@example.test>")
       (equal (mail-header-parse-address "User Name <user@example.test>")
              '("user@example.test" . "User Name"))
       (equal (mail-header-parse-addresses "One <one@example.test>, Two <two@example.test>")
              '(("one@example.test" . "One") ("two@example.test" . "Two")))
       (equal (mail-header-parse-address-lax "User Name user@example.test")
              '("user@example.test" . "User Name"))
       (equal (mail-header-parse-addresses-lax "User One <one@example.test>, Two User two@example.test")
              '(("one@example.test" . "User One") ("two@example.test" . "Two User")))))
EOF

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-ewoc-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((seen nil))
  (and (featurep 'ewoc)
       (fboundp 'ewoc-create)
       (fboundp 'ewoc-enter-last)
       (fboundp 'ewoc-enter-first)
       (fboundp 'ewoc-nth)
       (fboundp 'ewoc-data)
       (fboundp 'ewoc-set-data)
       (fboundp 'ewoc-map)
       (fboundp 'ewoc-delete)
       (with-temp-buffer
         (let ((ew (ewoc-create (lambda (x) (insert (format "[%s]\n" x))) "H\n" "F\n")))
           (ewoc-enter-last ew "b")
           (ewoc-enter-first ew "a")
           (let ((first (ewoc-nth ew 0))
                 (second (ewoc-nth ew 1)))
             (and first
                  second
                  (equal (ewoc-data first) "a")
                  (equal (ewoc-data second) "b")
                  (progn (ewoc-set-data second "c") t)
                  (progn (ewoc-map (lambda (x) (push x seen) nil) ew) t)
                  (member "a" seen)
                  (member "c" seen)
                  (progn (ewoc-delete ew first) t)
                  (not (string-match-p "\\[a\\]" (buffer-string)))
                  (string-match-p "H\n" (buffer-string))
                  (string-match-p "\\[c\\]" (buffer-string))
                  (string-match-p "F\n" (buffer-string))))))))
EOF

cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let ((ecomplete-database nil)
      (ecomplete-filter-regexp nil)
      (ecomplete-sort-predicate #'ecomplete-usage))
  (and (featurep 'ecomplete)
       (fboundp 'ecomplete-add-item)
       (fboundp 'ecomplete-get-item)
       (fboundp 'ecomplete-get-matches)
       (fboundp 'ecomplete--remove-item)
       (fboundp 'ecomplete-completion-table)
       (fboundp 'ecomplete-usage)
       (fboundp 'ecomplete-newness)
       (fboundp 'ecomplete-decay)
       (progn
         (ecomplete-add-item 'mail "alpha@example.test" "Alpha Example <alpha@example.test>")
         (ecomplete-add-item 'mail "beta@example.test" "Beta Example <beta@example.test>")
         (ecomplete-add-item 'mail "alpha@example.test" "Alpha Expanded <alpha@example.test>" t)
         t)
       (let ((item (ecomplete-get-item 'mail "alpha@example.test"))
             (matches (ecomplete-get-matches 'mail "Example")))
         (and item
              (= (cadr item) 2)
              (equal (cadddr item) "Alpha Expanded <alpha@example.test>")
              (string-match-p "Alpha Expanded" matches)
              (string-match-p "Beta Example" matches)))
       (let ((table (ecomplete-completion-table 'mail)))
         (member "Alpha Expanded <alpha@example.test>" (all-completions "Alpha" table)))
       (progn
         (ecomplete--remove-item 'mail "beta@example.test")
         (not (ecomplete-get-item 'mail "beta@example.test")))))
EOF

       (fboundp 'gv-get)

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-nadvice-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(defun nelisp-nadvice-proof-target (x) (+ x 1))
(defvar nelisp-nadvice-proof-seen nil)
(defun nelisp-nadvice-proof-before (&rest _args) (setq nelisp-nadvice-proof-seen t))
(defun nelisp-nadvice-proof-filter (ret) (* ret 10))
(setq nelisp-nadvice-proof-seen nil)
(and (featurep 'nadvice)
     (fboundp 'advice-add)
     (fboundp 'advice-remove)
     (fboundp 'advice-member-p)
     (fboundp 'advice-mapc)
     (fboundp 'advice-function-member-p)
     (macrop 'add-function)
     (macrop 'remove-function)
     (macrop 'define-advice)
     (progn
       (advice-add 'nelisp-nadvice-proof-target :before #'nelisp-nadvice-proof-before)
       (advice-add 'nelisp-nadvice-proof-target :filter-return #'nelisp-nadvice-proof-filter)
       t)
     (advice-member-p #'nelisp-nadvice-proof-before 'nelisp-nadvice-proof-target)
     (advice-member-p #'nelisp-nadvice-proof-filter 'nelisp-nadvice-proof-target)
     (= (nelisp-nadvice-proof-target 4) 50)
     nelisp-nadvice-proof-seen
     (progn
       (advice-remove 'nelisp-nadvice-proof-target #'nelisp-nadvice-proof-before)
       (advice-remove 'nelisp-nadvice-proof-target #'nelisp-nadvice-proof-filter)
       t)
     (not (advice-member-p #'nelisp-nadvice-proof-before 'nelisp-nadvice-proof-target))
     (= (nelisp-nadvice-proof-target 4) 5))
EOF
make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast \
  VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=180s \
  VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=150 \
  VENDOR_FAST_FILES="$(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/emacs-lisp/nadvice.el" \
  VENDOR_FAST_PROOF_FORM_FILE="$proof"
rm -f "$proof"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-regexp-opt-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(let* ((words (list "cat" "car" "dog" "door" "dot"))
       (re (regexp-opt words 'words))
       (plain (regexp-opt (list "alpha" "alpine" "beta")))
       (charset (regexp-opt-charset '(?a ?b ?c ?- ?]))))
  (and (featurep 'regexp-opt)
       (fboundp 'regexp-opt)
       (fboundp 'regexp-opt-depth)
       (fboundp 'regexp-opt-group)
       (fboundp 'regexp-opt-charset)
       (stringp re)
       (stringp plain)
       (stringp charset)
       (= (regexp-opt-depth "\\(a\\)\\(?:b\\)\\(c\\)") 2)
       (string-match-p re "cat")
       (string-match-p re "door")
       (not (string-match-p re "cow"))
       (string-match-p plain "alpha")
       (string-match-p plain "alpine")
       (string-match-p charset "a")
       (string-match-p charset "-")
       (string-match-p charset "]")
       (not (string-match-p charset "z"))))
EOF
make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast \
  VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=180s \
  VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=150 \
  VENDOR_FAST_FILES="$(pwd)/vendor/emacs-lisp/emacs-lisp/regexp-opt.el" \
  VENDOR_FAST_PROOF_FORM_FILE="$proof"
rm -f "$proof"

proof="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-pcase-proof.XXXXXX.el)"
cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(pcase-defmacro nelisp-pcase-proof-even ()
  '(pred (lambda (x) (= (% x 2) 0))))
(let* ((match1 (pcase '(tag 4 "ok")
                 (`(tag ,n ,s) (list n s))
                 (_ nil)))
       (match2 (pcase 8
                 ((nelisp-pcase-proof-even) 'even)
                 (_ 'odd)))
       (lambda-result (funcall (pcase-lambda (`(,a . ,b)) (+ a b)) '(2 . 5))))
  (pcase-let ((`(,x ,y) '(3 9)))
    (pcase-let* ((`(,head . ,tail) '(alpha beta gamma))
                 (`(,first-tail . ,rest-tail) tail))
      (and (featurep 'pcase)
           (macrop 'pcase)
           (macrop 'pcase-exhaustive)
           (macrop 'pcase-lambda)
           (macrop 'pcase-let)
           (macrop 'pcase-let*)
           (macrop 'pcase-dolist)
           (macrop 'pcase-setq)
           (macrop 'pcase-defmacro)
           (fboundp 'pcase--make-docstring)
           (equal match1 '(4 "ok"))
           (eq match2 'even)
           (= lambda-result 7)
           (= x 3)
           (= y 9)
           (eq head 'alpha)
           (eq first-tail 'beta)
           (equal rest-tail '(gamma))))))
EOF
make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast \

rm -f "$proof"

     (fboundp 'pcase--split-equal)
     (equal (pcase '(a . b) (`(,x . ,y) (list x y))) '(a b))
     (equal (pcase '(1 2 3) (`(1 ,x ,y) (+ x y))) 5)
     (equal (pcase 'foo ((or 'bar 'foo) 'ok) (_ 'bad)) 'ok)

prefix="$(mktemp /tmp/nelisp-pcase-prefix-47.XXXXXX.el)"
emacs --batch -Q --eval "
(with-temp-buffer
  (insert-file-contents \"vendor/emacs-lisp/emacs-lisp/pcase.el\")
  (goto-char (point-min))
  (let ((forms nil))
    (dotimes (_ 47)
      (push (read (current-buffer)) forms))
    (with-temp-file \"$prefix\"
      (dolist (form (nreverse forms))
        (prin1 form (current-buffer))
        (terpri (current-buffer))))))"

cat > "$proof" <<'EOF'
(defun nelisp-byte-run-proof-current (x) (+ x 1))
(define-obsolete-function-alias 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-old 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-current "30.1" "Proof obsolete alias.")
(defsubst nelisp-byte-run-proof-inline (x) (* x 2))
(make-obsolete-variable 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-old-var 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-new-var "30.1")
(define-obsolete-face-alias 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-old-face 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-new-face "30.1")
(let ((compile-value (eval-when-compile (+ 2 3)))
      (both-value (eval-and-compile (+ 4 5))))
  (and (macrop 'defsubst)
       (macrop 'define-obsolete-function-alias)
       (macrop 'define-obsolete-variable-alias)
       (macrop 'define-obsolete-face-alias)
       (macrop 'eval-when-compile)
       (macrop 'eval-and-compile)
       (fboundp 'make-obsolete)
       (fboundp 'make-obsolete-variable)
       (fboundp 'with-no-warnings)
       (fboundp 'set-advertised-calling-convention)
       (fboundp 'get-advertised-calling-convention)
       (= (nelisp-byte-run-proof-old 4) 5)
       (= (nelisp-byte-run-proof-inline 6) 12)
       (equal (get 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-old 'byte-obsolete-info)
              '(nelisp-byte-run-proof-current nil "30.1"))
       (equal (get 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-old-var 'byte-obsolete-variable)
              '(nelisp-byte-run-proof-new-var nil "30.1"))
       (eq (get 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-old-face 'face-alias)
           'nelisp-byte-run-proof-new-face)
       (equal (get 'nelisp-byte-run-proof-old-face 'obsolete-face) "30.1")
       (= compile-value 5)
       (= both-value 9)
       (= (with-no-warnings (+ 10 11)) 21)))
EOF
