225. Hollow-emission generator defect: the vendor replay generator
   emitted a BODY-LESS =(defmacro backquote (form))= that clobbered the
   standalone reader's own natively-baked =backquote= for the rest of
   the chain.  ROOT-CAUSED and FIXED in the generator, 2026-07-04.
   This is the proper, generator-side fix for the defect dev/nelisp
   merge =69301d56= diagnosed and worked around downstream (its
   =cold-image-org-e2e.sh= re-asserts a correct =backquote= after the
   chain; that workaround is now redundant but harmless).

   Symptom (as diagnosed in dev/nelisp =FINDINGS.md=): near the start of
   generated =.repl= chains, a body-less =(defmacro backquote (form))=
   redefines =backquote= as an always-nil macro; every backquote-built
   macro loaded afterwards (=org-with-wide-buffer=, =org-no-read-only=,
   ...) silently expands to nil, silently skipping large parts of Org
   initialization and driving =org-element-parse-buffer= into
   =(error nil)= (see items 223/224 correction notes).

   TRUE mechanism (corrects the hypothesis recorded in dev/nelisp
   =FINDINGS.md=): NOT byte-code body recovery.  FINDINGS.md guessed the
   generator "cannot recover a Lisp-readable body from host Emacs 30.1's
   compiled =backquote= byte-code object and silently emits an empty
   body"; in fact the generator never consults =symbol-function= at all
   -- it reads vendor/src source text form-by-form.  The real defect was
   a reader-quote HEAD COLLISION in the normalizer
   (=scripts/standalone-source-normalize.el=,
   =standalone-source-normalize-form=, pre-fix line 906, and the same
   pattern inside =standalone-source-normalize--backquote-datum=,
   pre-fix lines 887-893): any cons whose =car= was =backquote= / =\`=
   (or, inside backquote data, =comma= / =comma-at=) was treated as
   reader-emitted quote syntax =(HEAD DATUM)= and rebuilt as a
   TWO-ELEMENT list =(list HEAD (normalize DATUM))=.  The Lisp reader
   only ever emits that shape with exactly one trailing element, but the
   normalizer never checked the length.  So when the recursive walk over
   =(defmacro backquote (form) DOC BODY)= reached its cdr --
   =(backquote (form) DOC BODY)=, a 4-element list that merely SHARES a
   head symbol with backquote syntax -- it truncated it to
   =(backquote (form))=, reassembling as =(defmacro backquote (form))=:
   docstring and body silently dropped.  Any definition or code form
   literally named =backquote=/=comma=/=comma-at= in that cdr position
   would be hollowed the same way; the emission is deterministic for
   every source file that defines =backquote=.

   Enumeration (step-1 audit): regenerated the 68-file Org-chain =.repl=
   (item 222's =tmp-diag/org-chain-68-files-item222.txt=, host-side
   =vendor-repl-standalone--write-input=) and scanned every
   =defmacro=/=defun= emission for body-less shapes.  Result: exactly
   THREE hollow =(defmacro backquote (form))= emissions, all three from
   this one mechanism -- (1) the =src/emacs-backquote.el= polyfill chunk
   inside =build/nemacs-bootstrap.repl= (its guarded
   =(unless (fboundp 'backquote) (defmacro backquote (form) ...))=
   polyfill), and (2)+(3) the two =backquote= macro definitions in
   dev/nelisp's =scripts/nelisp-stdlib-prelude.el= (prelude replay,
   lines 1629 and 2703 upstream) -- plus ONE body-less
   =(defmacro sh-debug (&rest _args))= from vendor
   =progmodes/sh-script.el:1196=, which is NOT a defect: upstream
   Emacs's source is literally that body-less macro (a debug no-op), so
   the emission is faithful.  No other body-less defmacro/defun
   emissions exist in the chain.  =backquote= was therefore the only
   SYMPTOM, but the mechanism was general (any =backquote=-named
   definition through any chain), so a general fix was chosen over a
   name blacklist.

   Fix (general, shape-based; no skip-emission needed because the body
   was never actually unrecoverable): new predicate
   =standalone-source-normalize--reader-quote-form-p=
   (=scripts/standalone-source-normalize.el:883=) requires the exact
   two-element =(HEAD DATUM)= shape before the reader-quote fast path
   fires; =standalone-source-normalize-form= (now line 924) and
   =standalone-source-normalize--backquote-datum= (now line 903) use it
   for =backquote=/=\`= and =comma=/=comma-at=/=\,=/=\,@= heads.  Longer
   lists that merely share a head symbol now take the ordinary
   recursive-walk path and survive intact:
   =(defmacro backquote (form) "doc" (emacs-backquote--expand form))=
   round-trips unchanged.  Also bumped
   =standalone-source-normalize-cache-version= 128 -> 129: the
   normalized-form cache keys only on source truename/mtime/size, so
   without the bump, stale pre-fix cache entries kept re-serving the
   hollow forms (observed live: the first post-fix gate run's kept
   =.repl= still had the two prelude hollows from a Jul 1 cache).

   Regression tests: three new ERTs in
   =test/standalone-source-normalize-test.el=
   (=normalizes-genuine-backquote-data=,
   =preserves-defmacro-named-backquote=,
   =preserves-defun-named-backquote-in-guard=); suite 135/135 PASS
   (was 132), =standalone-diagnostics-test.el= 32/32 PASS,
   =make test-fast= 1073 tests with the same 6 known failures (four
   =emacs-redisplay-test= + =Info-find-file=), no new failures.

   Verification: regenerated =build/nemacs-bootstrap.{el,repl}= (the
   =src/emacs-backquote.el= chunk now carries the full guarded polyfill
   body) and the 68-file Org-chain =.repl= -- zero body-less emissions
   remain (only the faithful upstream =sh-debug= no-op).  Trustworthy
   gate (=make diagnose-vendor-repl-replay-fast=,
   =VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=900s= =VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=860=

   (fboundp 'org-element-parse-buffer) (commandp 'org-mode)
   (eq (backquote 42) 42))=
   (=tmp-diag/proof-item225-org-chain-plus-backquote.el=): status=done,
   exit=0, sentinel =VENDOR-REPL-STANDALONE=ok=, twice -- first run
   439.2 s (whose kept =.repl= still carried the two stale-cache prelude

   zero body-less emissions, prelude/bootstrap =backquote= definitions

226. =define-derived-mode= cleanup-arm workaround retired for child
   bodies, 2026-07-05.  ROOT CAUSE of the workaround: commit
   =7b0d034= put the generated child mode transition, body, and hook
   call in the cleanup arm of an =unwind-protect= because standalone
   NeLisp was losing forms that followed macro-generated parent
   major-mode calls, especially nested =outline-mode= derived modes.
   The later item 221 fix repaired the backquote-template macro
   invocation / command-install symptom that had made generated derived
   modes fail the =fboundp= + =commandp= gates, and the item 225
   reader-quote fix repaired hollowed =backquote= definitions.  However,
   cold-image activation still shows a remaining parent-continuation
   line-drop when =outline-mode= or =org-mode= is called from a temp
   buffer, so the original parent-call continuation defect is not fully
   fixed on that path.

   Fix shape: =src/emacs-mode.el= now matches upstream
   =derived.el='s observable ordering for the child body: call the
   parent first, then identify the child major mode, run the BODY as
   ordinary sequential forms, and run mode hooks at the end.  The child
   BODY and hook call are no longer in an =unwind-protect= cleanup arm.
   To avoid reintroducing the cold-image parent-continuation drop, only
   the parent call remains wrapped in a small =unwind-protect= protected
   form with an empty cleanup and a completion flag; if the parent does
   not return, the generated mode signals =emacs-mode-error= instead of
   running the child body from cleanup.  This keeps the workaround away
   from command semantics and buffer mutation performed by child bodies.

   Regression coverage: =test/emacs-mode-builtins-test.el= adds a
   nested derived-mode sequencing test proving parent body, child body,
   and child hook order.  Focused host ERT for the touched module:
   19/19 PASS.  =make test-fast=: 1073 tests, 1067 expected, the same
   6 known failures only (=emacs-redisplay-test= x5 including the two
   core matrix/paint tests, plus the vendor-first =Info-find-file=
   failure); no new failures.  The generated package scaffold was
   refreshed so =packages/nelisp-emacs-core/lisp/emacs-mode.el= carries
   the same bridge implementation as =src/emacs-mode.el=.

   Trustworthy replay gate, one standalone reader at a time, warm
   =build/standalone-source-cache=, =VENDOR_REPL_TIMEOUT=900s= and
   =VENDOR_REPL_INTERNAL_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=860=: magit-base 7-file chain
   with =(and (fboundp 'magit-section-mode)
   (commandp 'magit-section-mode))=, status=done, exit=0, 118.39 s;
   text-mode strong proof, status=done, exit=0, 44.08 s; Org chain used
   the preserved 68-file reconstruction from item 222 because the exact
   item 215/221 61-file list was previously lost, with the 5-conjunct
   Org proof plus live =backquote= check
   =(and (featurep 'org) (featurep 'org-element) (fboundp 'org-mode)
   (fboundp 'org-element-parse-buffer) (commandp 'org-mode)
   (eq (backquote 42) 42))=, status=done, exit=0, 350.70 s.

   Cold-image result after regenerating =build/nemacs-bootstrap.repl=:
   the clone's gate-prelude image build still segfaults during
   replay-load (exit 139) before dump.  The default-prelude cold image
   builds from this repo's regenerated bootstrap and boots faithfully:
   replay-load 6.775 s, dump 0.558 s, cold boot 0.651 s, cold-boot peak
   RSS 532740 KB, faithfulness =(t t t t (interactive) t)=.  The
   requested temp-buffer probes no longer show the cleanup-arm blowup
   (both complete in 0.718 s with about 1.5 MB probe-side peak RSS), but
   they do not yet produce the target values: =(with-temp-buffer
   (org-mode) major-mode)= exits 0 with blank stdout, and
   =(with-temp-buffer (insert "* h") (org-mode)
   (if (org-element-parse-buffer) 'OK 'NIL))= exits 0 with blank
   stdout.  Marker probes show the activation line itself is still
   silently dropped before the after-marker for both =outline-mode= and
   =org-mode=.  Conclusion: the structural cleanup-arm body blowup has
   been removed, but a separate cold-image parent activation/line-drop
   defect remains.

227. Invisibility-spec compat setters ported for in-buffer Org activation,
   2026-07-05.  Root cause from item 226 follow-up: upstream
   =outline-mode= and =org-mode= mode bodies call
   =add-to-invisibility-spec=, but the NeLisp buffer-core bridge had only
   =buffer-invisibility-spec= and the read-side =invisible-p= analog.
   The missing unprefixed compatibility functions made real mode
   activation abort with =void-function add-to-invisibility-spec= once REPL
   diagnostics became visible.

   Fix shape: =src/emacs-buffer-builtins.el= now provides
   =emacs-buffer-builtins-add-to-invisibility-spec= and
   =emacs-buffer-builtins-remove-from-invisibility-spec=, with
   =add-to-invisibility-spec= / =remove-from-invisibility-spec= aliases
   installed only through the existing standalone-or-missing builtin gate.
   The list semantics match upstream =subr.el=: adding to =t= first turns
   the spec into =(t)= before consing the new element, and removal uses
   =delete= for list specs or =(t)= for non-list specs.  Because the
   standalone buffer substrate does not intercept ordinary =setq= for
   buffer-local variables, the setter path writes through
   =emacs-buffer-set-buffer-local-value= when a NeLisp current buffer
   exists; host Emacs keeps ordinary =setq= semantics.  The read-side
   =invisible-p= helper now reads the current buffer's local
   =buffer-invisibility-spec= value when present.

   Regression coverage: =test/emacs-buffer-builtins-test.el= adds
   add/remove coverage for atom entries and =(SYMBOL . ELLIPSIS)= cons
   entries, plus a temp-buffer locality check proving one buffer's
   invisibility spec does not leak to another.  Focused Host ERT:
   =emacs-buffer-builtins-test/invisibility-spec= 2/2 PASS.  Full
   =test/emacs-buffer-builtins-test.el=: 41/41 PASS.  =make test-fast=:
   1075 tests, 1069 expected, the same 6 known failures only
   (=emacs-redisplay-test= x5 and
   =vendor-first-core-modes-test/lightweight-support-libraries-load-vendor-source=
   with =void-function Info-find-file=); no new failures.

   Generated artifacts: =make nemacs-library-package-scaffold
   build-nelisp-bootstrap= refreshed
   =packages/nelisp-emacs-buffer-core/lisp/emacs-buffer-builtins.el= and
   regenerated =build/nemacs-bootstrap.repl= so the bridge ships to the
   standalone reader replay.

   Cold-image e2e with the diagnostics reader from
   =/home/madblack-21/Cowork/Notes/dev/nelisp.clone-capture= at
   =440cdfb7=, =NELISP_E2E_KEEP=1=, one run, then workdir deleted:
   replay-load 6.729 s, dump 0.531 s, cold boot 0.519 s, cold-boot peak
   RSS 513408 KB, faithfulness =(t t t t (interactive) t)= identical.
   Probe (a), exact form =(with-temp-buffer (outline-mode) (prin1
   major-mode))=, timeout 30, RSS abort 8 GiB, one reader: exit 0,
   killed=none, wall 532 ms, peak RSS 513860 KB, stdout empty, stderr
   exactly =nelisp: uncaught error: void-variable: (paragraph-start)=.
   Probe (b), exact form =(with-temp-buffer (org-mode) (prin1
   major-mode))=, timeout 120, RSS abort 8 GiB, one reader: exit 0,
   killed=none, wall 534 ms, peak RSS 513872 KB, stdout empty, stderr
   exactly =nelisp: uncaught error: void-variable: (paragraph-start)=.
   Probe (c) was not run because (b) did not print =org-mode=.  This
   confirms the invisibility-spec blocker is removed and exposes the next
   activation blocker as =paragraph-start=, not chased in this item.

   Gate sanity: the preserved 68-file Org-chain proof from item 222
   (=tmp-diag/org-chain-68-files-item222.txt=) with item 225's

228. Paragraph regexp defaults ported for in-buffer Org activation,
   2026-07-05.  Iteration log: =paragraph-start= / =paragraph-separate=
   -> commit =433ee459= ("Port paragraph defaults for org activation")
   -> probe delta: the previous visible
   =void-variable: (paragraph-start)= blocker disappeared, but the next
   result is a reader-level segmentation fault rather than another simple
   missing symbol.

   Fix shape: =src/emacs-textmodes-stub.el= now defines the upstream
   =textmodes/paragraphs.el= defaults when absent:
   =paragraph-start= as ="\f\\|[ \t]*$"= and
   =paragraph-separate= as ="[ \t\f]*$"=.  The generated scaffold copy
   =packages/nelisp-emacs-textmodes-stub/lisp/emacs-textmodes-stub.el=
   was refreshed by =make nemacs-library-package-scaffold
   build-nelisp-bootstrap=.  The module also registers both variables
   through =make-variable-buffer-local= on standalone/missing-host
   runtimes.  Focused host ERT for the owning module:
   =test/emacs-textmodes-stub-test.el= 13/13 PASS.

   Cold-image e2e with the diagnostics reader from
